      # Symlink chromium-browser to chromium for compatibility with many test runners
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      # Clean up
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy package.json and package-lock.json first for Docker layer caching
  COPY package.json package-lock.json* ./
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci

  COPY . .

        python3-pip \

  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .

  RUN npm ci

  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb to enable headless browser tests
  CMD [ "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test" ]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM node:18-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # Install system dependencies: git, chromium, firefox, and other dev tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        git \
        ca-certificates \
        curl \
        wget \
        gnupg \
        build-essential \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        chromium \
        chromium-driver \
        firefox-esr \
        xvfb \
        xauth \
        fonts-liberation \
        libappindicator3-1 \
        libasound2 \
        libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
        libatk1.0-0 \
        libcups2 \
        libdbus-1-3 \
        libdrm2 \
        libgbm1 \
        libgtk-3-0 \
        libnspr4 \
        libnss3 \
        libx11-xcb1 \
        libxcomposite1 \
        libxdamage1 \
        libxrandr2 \
        libxss1 \
        libxtst6 \
        lsb-release \
        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # By default, use a non-root user for security (optional, uncomment if needed)
  # RUN useradd -m cc && chown -R cc:cc /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # USER cc
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb to enable headless browser tests
  CMD [ "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test" ]

      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout and verbose output
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug"]

      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for debugging
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "node", "--trace-warnings", "node_modules/.bin/npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug"]

  FROM node:18-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # Install system dependencies: git, chromium, firefox, and other dev tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        git \
        ca-certificates \
        curl \
        wget \
        gnupg \
        build-essential \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        chromium \
        chromium-driver \
        firefox-esr \
        xvfb \
        xauth \
        fonts-liberation \
        libappindicator3-1 \
        libasound2 \
        libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
        libatk1.0-0 \
        libcups2 \
        libdbus-1-3 \
        libdrm2 \
        libgbm1 \
        libgtk-3-0 \
        libnspr4 \
        libnss3 \
        libx11-xcb1 \
        libxcomposite1 \
        libxdamage1 \
        libxrandr2 \
        libxss1 \
        libxtst6 \
        lsb-release \
        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for debugging
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug"]

  next step

    - If tests spin up a local HTTP server, ensure all async setup/teardown is correctly awaited.

  - Optionally, add `RUN node --trace-warnings node_modules/.bin/npm test -- --dry-run` after `npm run build` in the Dockerfile to catch warnings/errors during test discovery without running full tests.
  - If warnings about `buffer.File` are problematic, audit dependencies for use of experimental APIs and update or patch as appropriate.
  - Add documentation in README/CONTRIBUTING.md if certain tests require network access or specific ports, in alignment with the setup plan.

  #### 1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED
  - **Node.js**:  
    - Use official Node.js Linux x64 (amd64) binaries or Docker images (e.g., node:18-bullseye or node:20-bookworm).
    - Do not use ARM or ARM64 images (no aarch64/arm64).
    - Minimum: Node.js v10+, Recommended: v18.x or higher for best compatibility.
    - If using Docker, specify `--platform=linux/amd64` if running on multi-arch host.
  - **npm** (bundled with Node.js) or **yarn**, **pnpm**, or **bun**:  
    - All supported on x86_64 Linux.
    - No platform-specific caveats; choose npm (default, pre-installed with Node.js).
  - **Git, Gulp, Rollup, Webpack, etc.**:  
    - All open-source tools available for Linux x86_64.
    - No hardware-specific limitations.
    - Use apt, dnf, yum, or as devDependencies in package.json as appropriate.
    - All npm packages listed are platform-independent.
  - **Bower**: (Optional, for legacy browser support)  
    - Available for Linux x86_64 via npm.
  - **Browsers for Karma**:  
    - On Linux, install via apt:
        - Chrome: Use Google Chrome or Chromium for karma-chrome-launcher.
        - Firefox: Use official Firefox.

  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build

  RUN node --trace-warnings node_modules/.bin/npm test -- --dry-run || true
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug

  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for deeper diagnostics
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug", "--trace-warnings"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM node:18-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # Install system dependencies: git, chromium, firefox, and other dev tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        git \
        ca-certificates \
        curl \
        wget \
        gnupg \
        build-essential \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        chromium \
        chromium-driver \
        firefox-esr \
        xvfb \
        xauth \
        fonts-liberation \
        libappindicator3-1 \
        libasound2 \
        libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
        libatk1.0-0 \
        libcups2 \
        libdbus-1-3 \
        libdrm2 \
        libgbm1 \
        libgtk-3-0 \
        libnspr4 \
        libnss3 \
        libx11-xcb1 \
        libxcomposite1 \
        libxdamage1 \
        libxrandr2 \
        libxss1 \
        libxtst6 \
        lsb-release \
        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # Dry-run the test runner to catch warnings/errors in test discovery, fail build on error
  RUN node --trace-warnings node_modules/.bin/npm test -- --dry-run
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Set OpenSSL legacy provider only if absolutely needed (uncomment if required)
  # ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max_old_space_size=4096 --openssl-legacy-provider"
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for deeper diagnostics
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "node", "--trace-warnings", "node_modules/.bin/npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug"]

        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # Dry-run the test runner to catch warnings/errors in test discovery, fail build on error
  RUN npm test -- --dry-run || echo "Test dry-run failed, continuing build for further isolation"
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Set OpenSSL legacy provider only if absolutely needed (uncomment if required)
  # ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max_old_space_size=4096 --openssl-legacy-provider"
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for deeper diagnostics
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "node", "--trace-warnings", "node_modules/.bin/npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug"]

  FROM node:18-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # Install system dependencies: git, chromium, firefox, and other dev tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        git \
        ca-certificates \
        curl \
        wget \
        gnupg \
        build-essential \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        chromium \
        chromium-driver \
        firefox-esr \
        xvfb \
        xauth \
        fonts-liberation \
        libappindicator3-1 \
        libasound2 \
        libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
        libatk1.0-0 \
        libcups2 \
        libdbus-1-3 \
        libdrm2 \
        libgbm1 \
        libgtk-3-0 \
        libnspr4 \
        libnss3 \
        libx11-xcb1 \
        libxcomposite1 \
        libxdamage1 \
        libxrandr2 \
        libxss1 \
        libxtst6 \
        lsb-release \
        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # Dry-run the test runner to catch warnings/errors in test discovery, fail build on error
  RUN npm test -- --dry-run || echo "Test dry-run failed, continuing build for further isolation"
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Set OpenSSL legacy provider only if absolutely needed (uncomment if required)
  # ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--max_old_space_size=4096 --openssl-legacy-provider"
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for deeper diagnostics
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug"]

  FROM node:18-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # Install system dependencies: git, chromium, firefox, and other dev tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        git \
        ca-certificates \
        curl \
        wget \
        gnupg \
        build-essential \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        chromium \
        chromium-driver \
        firefox-esr \
        xvfb \
        xauth \
        fonts-liberation \
        libappindicator3-1 \
        libasound2 \
        libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
        libatk1.0-0 \
        libcups2 \
        libdbus-1-3 \
        libdrm2 \
        libgbm1 \
        libgtk-3-0 \
        libnspr4 \
        libnss3 \
        libx11-xcb1 \
        libxcomposite1 \
        libxdamage1 \
        libxrandr2 \
        libxss1 \
        libxtst6 \
        lsb-release \
        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # Dry-run the test runner to catch warnings/errors in test discovery, fail build on error
  RUN npm test -- --dry-run || echo "Test dry-run failed, continuing build for further isolation"
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Expose commonly-used test ports for HTTP servers, update as needed for test/server code
  EXPOSE 3000 4000 9876
  # Add more logging and debugging for test server/network issues
  ENV DEBUG=axios:*,test,server
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for deeper diagnostics
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug", "--trace-warnings"]

  FROM node:18-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # Install system dependencies: git, chromium, firefox, and other dev tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        git \
        ca-certificates \
        curl \
        wget \
        gnupg \
        build-essential \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        chromium \
        chromium-driver \
        firefox-esr \
        xvfb \
        xauth \
        fonts-liberation \
        libappindicator3-1 \
        libasound2 \
        libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
        libatk1.0-0 \
        libcups2 \
        libdbus-1-3 \
        libdrm2 \
        libgbm1 \
        libgtk-3-0 \
        libnspr4 \
        libnss3 \
        libx11-xcb1 \
        libxcomposite1 \
        libxdamage1 \
        libxrandr2 \
        libxss1 \
        libxtst6 \
        lsb-release \
        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # Early test run, fail build if it fails (for earlier detection)
  RUN npm test -- --single-run --log-level debug --trace-warnings
  # Dry-run the test runner to catch warnings/errors in test discovery, fail build on error
  RUN npm test -- --dry-run || echo "Test dry-run failed, continuing build for further isolation"
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Expose commonly-used test ports for HTTP servers, update as needed for test/server code
  EXPOSE 3000 4000 9876
  # Add more logging and debugging for test server/network issues
  ENV DEBUG=axios:*,test,server
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for deeper diagnostics
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "node", "--trace-warnings", "$(which npm)", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug", "--trace-warnings"]

  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them

  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # (TEMPORARILY DISABLED) Early test run -- comment out for debugging build failures
  # RUN npm test -- --single-run --log-level debug --trace-warnings

  # RUN npm test -- --dry-run || echo "Test dry-run failed, continuing build for further isolation"
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Expose commonly-used test ports for HTTP servers, update as needed for test/server code
  EXPOSE 3000 4000 9876

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM node:18-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/axios_axios
  # Install system dependencies: git, chromium, firefox, and other dev tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
        git \
        ca-certificates \
        curl \
        wget \
        gnupg \
        build-essential \
        python3 \
        python3-pip \
        chromium \
        chromium-driver \
        firefox-esr \
        xvfb \
        xauth \
        fonts-liberation \
        libappindicator3-1 \
        libasound2 \
        libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
        libatk1.0-0 \
        libcups2 \
        libdbus-1-3 \
        libdrm2 \
        libgbm1 \
        libgtk-3-0 \
        libnspr4 \
        libnss3 \
        libx11-xcb1 \
        libxcomposite1 \
        libxdamage1 \
        libxrandr2 \
        libxss1 \
        libxtst6 \
        lsb-release \
        xdg-utils \
        --no-install-suggests && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/chromium /usr/bin/chromium-browser && \
      apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Optionally install Bower globally (for legacy browser support)
  RUN npm install -g bower
  # Copy all files (including husky and hooks) before npm ci so scripts can find them
  COPY . .
  # Install NPM dependencies
  RUN npm ci
  # Build the project before running tests (if required for tests)
  RUN npm run build
  # (TEMPORARILY DISABLED) Early test run -- comment out for debugging build failures
  # RUN npm test -- --single-run --log-level debug --trace-warnings
  # (TEMPORARILY DISABLED) Dry-run the test runner -- comment out for debugging build failures
  # RUN npm test -- --dry-run || echo "Test dry-run failed, continuing build for further isolation"
  # Set environment variable for headless browser testing (Karma, Chromium, Firefox)
  ENV CHROME_BIN=/usr/bin/chromium \
      FIREFOX_BIN=/usr/bin/firefox
  # Increase node and test process timeout, add more verbosity to help debug
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS=--max_old_space_size=4096
  # Expose commonly-used test ports for HTTP servers, update as needed for test/server code
  EXPOSE 3000 4000 9876
  # Add more logging and debugging for test server/network issues
  ENV DEBUG=axios:*,test,server
  # Default command: Run tests under Xvfb with a 20-minute timeout, verbose output, and trace warnings for deeper diagnostics
  CMD ["timeout", "20m", "xvfb-run", "-a", "npm", "test", "--", "--single-run", "--log-level", "debug", "--trace-warnings"]
